METABOLITES THE GEL LEAKED PROFUSELY THROUGH MULTIPLE PERFORATIONS THE GEL WAS ALSO INVASIVE AND OF AN EASILY DISPERSED NATURE THE LOSS OF GEL PROPERTY REVERSION FROM A COHESIVE PRODUCT TO AN OIL-LIKE
